# <a name="release-notes-for-office-insiders"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-103">Office 測試人員的版本資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-103">Release Notes for Office Insiders</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-104">本文包含 Windows 電腦版 Word、Excel、PowerPoint、Outlook、Access 和 Project 測試人員組建的版本資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-104">This article contains release notes for Insider builds of Word, Excel, PowerPoint, Outlook, Access, and Project for Windows desktop.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-105">我們每週都強調有趣的新功能、重要修正，以及我們想讓您知道的重大問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-105">Every week, we’ll highlight interesting new features, important fixes, and any significant issues we want you to know about.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-106">請注意，我們在一段時間內會經常推出新功能 (某些時候還有修正) 給測試人員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-106">Note that we often roll out features (and sometimes even fixes) to Insiders over a period of time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-107">這樣可讓我們確保功能都運作順利，然後才推出給更廣泛的對象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-107">This allows us to ensure that things are working smoothly before releasing the feature to a wider audience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-108">所以，如果你沒有看到下面描述的項目，不要擔心你最終會得到它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-108">So, if you don’t see something described below, don't worry you'll get it eventually.</span></span>  

> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="62973-109">版本資訊會每週發佈，可能是多個組建的編譯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-109">Release notes are posted weekly and may be a compilation of multiple builds.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="62973-110">版本資訊發佈日期可能與實際組建發行日期不相符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-110">The release notes publication date may not match the actual build release date.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="62973-111">現有 Office 365 專業增強版安裝上的 Microsoft Teams - 從 6 月底開始，Microsoft Teams 將在更新這些安裝時，新增至 Office 365 專業增強版的 (和 Office 365 商務版) 的現有安裝中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-111">Microsoft Teams on existing installations of Office 365 ProPlus - Beginning in late June, Microsoft Teams will be included in existing installations of Office 365 ProPlus (and Office 365 Business) upon updates of these installations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-112">新增 Teams 的日期取決於您使用的更新通道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-112">The date when Teams will be added depends on which update channel you're using.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-113">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[隨著 Office 365 專業增強版部署 Microsoft Teams](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployoffice/teams-install)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-113">Please refer to [Deploy Microsoft Teams with Office 365 ProPlus](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployoffice/teams-install) for additional information.</span></span>

[//]: # (DO NOT REMOVE)

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-118">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-118">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-119">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-119">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="62973-120">**即時讀取與回覆：** 直接從電子郵件回覆註解和提及，而不需開啟活頁簿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-120">**Read and reply on the fly:** Respond to comments and mentions right from email without opening the workbook.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-123">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-123">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-124">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-124">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="62973-125">修正根據保留原則到期的電子郵件會顯示兩個標籤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-125">Fixed an issue where emails expiring based on a retention policy would display two labels.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-126">其中一個顯示郵件將在一天內過期，另一個則顯示將在兩天內到期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-126">One showing that the mail will expire in one day and another displaying that it will expire in two days.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-127">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-127">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="62973-128">修正在具有「反轉」頁面色彩的閱讀模式中，備註提示未顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-128">Fixed an issue where comment hint was not visible in read mode with &quot;Inverse&quot; page color.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="62973-129">修正在編輯備註之後將文字設為斜體然後再張貼，斜體格式設定遺失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-129">Fixed an issue where italics formatting is lost after editing a comment, italicizing the text and then posting it.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="62973-130">修正備註內容功能表中的備註命令 (編輯備註、回覆備註、刪除備註、解決備註) 未顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-130">Fixed an issue where comment commands (Edit comment, Reply to comment, Delete comment, Resolve comment) in the comments context menu were not being displayed.</span></span>

[//]: # (DO NOT REMOVE BUGDETAILS CONTENT END)

## <a name="version-2001-january-03"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-174">版本 2001：1 月 3 日</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-174">Version 2001: January 03</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="62973-175">*版本 2001 (組建 12425.20000)*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-175">*Version 2001 (Build 12425.20000)*</span></span>

[//]: # (DO NOT REMOVE BUGDETAILS CONTENT START)

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-177">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-177">Resolved issues</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-178">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-178">Excel</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="62973-179">有些框線在 A4 大小的紙張上可能無法如預期列印。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-179">Some border lines may not print as expected on A4 size paper.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="62973-180">使用 VBA 將影像新增到工作表圖表物件的頁首/頁尾可能會導致錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-180">Adding an image to the header/footer of a chart object on a sheet using VBA may result in an error.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="62973-181">設定圖表座標軸格式時，標籤之間的間隔限制為 255。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-181">When formatting a chart axis, the interval between labels was limited to 255.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="62973-182">已修正嘗試重新整理 XML 查詢 (資料來源 URL 遭截斷) 時發生錯誤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-182">Fixed an issue where an error would occur trying to refresh an XML query in which the URL to the datasource was being truncated.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="62973-183">活頁簿統計資料會報告所有開啟的活頁簿 (包括個人巨集活頁簿) 中的巨集計數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-183">Workbook Statistics would report a macro count from all open workbooks, including the personal macro workbook.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-184">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-184">Outlook</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="62973-185">切換資料夾可能會導致郵件清單/郵件預覽中「快閃」短暫的空白。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-185">Switching folders may result in a brief white 'flash' in the mail list / mail preview.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-186">此行為在深色模式中更明顯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-186">This behavior was more pronounced in dark mode.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-187">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-187">PowerPoint</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="62973-188">已修正呼叫 Shape.Paste 方法會導致貼上的圖形置於焦點下的物件模型問題。&nbsp;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-188">Fixed an Object Model issue where calling Shape.Paste method would result in the pasted shape receiving focus.&nbsp;</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="62973-189">已改善複製貼上案例：&nbsp;以程式設計方式從 PowerPoint 投影片複製圖形，並將其貼到循環播放中的另一張投影片會失敗並發生異常錯誤。&nbsp;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-189">Improved a copy-paste scenario:&nbsp;Progamatically copying a shape from a PowerPoint slide and pasting it to another slide in a loop could fail with an exception error.&nbsp;</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="62973-190">折疊及展開節標頭後，投影片節標頭的動畫無法正確呈現。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-190">Animation in the section headers of slides would not render properly after collapsing and expanding section headers.</span></span>

### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-191">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-191">Project</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="62973-192">已修正文字換行在任務和資源使用狀況檢視中無法正常運作的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-192">Fixed an issue where text wrapping wasn't working in the task and resource usage views.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="62973-193">已修正如果某資源有多個成本比率，則工作分派的成本值可能不正確的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-193">Fixed an issue where if a resource has more than one cost rate, cost value on assignments may not be correct.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-194">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-194">Word</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="62973-195">在方程式中插入控制項 (例如文字內容控制項)，然後儲存再開啟檔案，便會導致內容無法讀取的錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-195">Inserting a control (such as a Text Content Control) in an equation, then saving and opening the file would result in an un-readable content error.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="62973-196">共同撰寫時，Word 電腦版可能不會顯示使用 Word Online 新增註解的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-196">When co-authoring, adding a comment using Word online may not appear in Word desktop.</span></span>

#### <a name="dark-mode-for-black-theme-in-outlook-desktop"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-888">Outlook 電腦版中用於黑色佈景主題的深色模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-888">Dark Mode for Black Theme in Outlook Desktop</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="62973-897">在深色模式中撰寫電子郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-897">Compose emails in dark mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-898">使用功能區中的太陽切換，預覽您的郵件使用淺色背景時的外觀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-898">Preview what your message will look like with a light background by using the sun toggle in the ribbon.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="62973-899">如果您遇到未正確顯示的任何電子郵件，請將其 (當作附件) 傳送到 OutlookDarkModeFail@service.microsoft.com</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-899">If you encounter any emails that don't render properly, please send them (as an attachment) to OutlookDarkModeFail@service.microsoft.com</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-982">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-982">Word</span></span>

#### <a name="open-document-links-in-word"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-983">在 Word 中開啟文件連結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-983">Open document links in Word</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-984">當您在 Office 中按一下文件連結時，您可以更新您的喜好設定，以預設在 Word App 中開啟該連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-984">When you click a document link in Office, you can update your preference to open in the Word app by default.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="62973-985">若要更新您的喜好設定，請移至 [檔案] -> [選項] -> [進階] -> [連結處理]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-985">To update your preference go to File->Options->Advanced->Link Handling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-986">深入了解：https://support.office.com/article/open-file-links-directly-in-office-desktop-apps-fe241745-9e05-4142-9ba8-1bb1dc044773?ui=en-US&rs=en-US&ad=US</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-986">Learn more: https://support.office.com/article/open-file-links-directly-in-office-desktop-apps-fe241745-9e05-4142-9ba8-1bb1dc044773?ui=en-US&rs=en-US&ad=US</span></span>

##### <a name="getting-started"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-987">開始使用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-987">Getting Started:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-988">此功能將預設為關閉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-988">Feature will default to off.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-989">使用者可以透過 [選項] -> [進階] -> [連結處理] 設定來開啟它，也可以在 Win32 WXP 應用程式帶他們進行選擇加入體驗時選擇加入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-989">Users can either turn it on via Options->Advanced->Link Handling setting, or they can opt-in when Win32 WXP apps take them through an opt-in experience.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="62973-990">當使用者按一下透過 Outlook/Word/PowerPoint/Excel 儲存在 OneDrive/商務用 OneDrive/SharePoint 上的 Word/PowerPoint/Excel 檔案時，這些連結依預設會在適當的 Office 應用程式中 (而非瀏覽器中) 開啟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-990">When users click on links to Word/PowerPoint/Excel files stored on OneDrive/OneDrive for Business/SharePoint from Outlook/Word/PowerPoint/Excel, these links will open in the appropriate Office application instead of the browser by default.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-991">若要變更此預設值，使用者可以更新 Outlook/Word/Excel/PowerPoint 中的下列設定：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-991">To change this default, users can update the following setting in Outlook/Word/Excel/PowerPoint:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-992">[檔案] -> [選項] -> [進階] -> [連結處理]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-992">File->Options->Advanced->Link Handling</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-993">此設定會在 Outlook/Word/PowerPoint/Excel 之間共用，而且可以在任一應用程式中設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-993">This setting is shared across Outlook/Word/PowerPoint/Excel and can be set in any of these apps.</span></span>

##### <a name="scenarios-to-try"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-994">可嘗試使用的案例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-994">Scenarios to Try:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-995">若要觸發選擇加入體驗 - 從 Outlook/Word/PowerPoint/Excel 開啟儲存在 OneDrive/SharePoint 中 Word 文件的連結 - 按一下 [在來自 Office Online 的用戶端中開啟] - 在 30 天內執行此動作兩次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-995">To trigger the opt-in experience - Open a link tot a Word document stored in OneDrive/SharePoint from Outlook/Word/PowerPoint/Excel - click on Open in Client from Office Online - do this twice in a 30 day window.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-996">在您選擇加入之後，依預設會在 Win32 應用程式中啟動連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-996">After you opt-in, links will launch in the Win32 apps by default.</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-1012">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1012">Excel</span></span>

#### <a name="open-workbook-links-in-excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-1013">在 Excel 中開啟活頁簿連結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1013">Open workbook links in Excel</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-1014">當您在 Office 中按一下活頁簿連結時，您可以更新您的喜好設定，以預設在 Excel App 中開啟該連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1014">When you click a workbook link in Office, you can update your preference to open in the Excel app by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-1015">若要更新您的喜好設定，請移至 [檔案] -> [選項] -> [進階] -> [連結處理]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1015">To update your preference, go to File->Options->Advanced->Link Handling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-1016">深入了解：https://support.office.com/article/open-file-links-directly-in-office-desktop-apps-fe241745-9e05-4142-9ba8-1bb1dc044773?ui=en-US&rs=en-US&ad=US</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1016">Learn More: https://support.office.com/article/open-file-links-directly-in-office-desktop-apps-fe241745-9e05-4142-9ba8-1bb1dc044773?ui=en-US&rs=en-US&ad=US</span></span>

##### <a name="getting-started"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-1017">開始使用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1017">Getting Started:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-1018">此功能將預設為關閉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1018">Feature will default to off.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-1019">使用者可以透過 [選項] -> [進階] -> [連結處理] 設定來開啟它，也可以在 Win32 WXP 應用程式帶他們進行選擇加入體驗時選擇加入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1019">Users can either turn it on via Options->Advanced->Link Handling setting, or they can opt-in when Win32 WXP apps take them through an opt-in experience.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="62973-1020">當使用者按一下透過 Outlook/Word/PowerPoint/Excel 儲存在 OneDrive/商務用 OneDrive/SharePoint 上的 Word/PowerPoint/Excel 檔案時，這些連結依預設會在適當的 Office 應用程式中 (而非瀏覽器中) 開啟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1020">When users click on links to Word/PowerPoint/Excel files stored on OneDrive/OneDrive for Business/SharePoint from Outlook/Word/PowerPoint/Excel, these links will open in the appropriate Office application instead of the browser by default.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-1021">若要變更此預設值，使用者可以更新 Outlook/Word/Excel/PowerPoint 中的下列設定：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1021">To change this default, users can update the following setting in Outlook/Word/Excel/PowerPoint:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-1022">[檔案] -> [選項] -> [進階] -> [連結處理]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1022">File->Options->Advanced->Link Handling</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-1023">此設定會在 Outlook/Word/PowerPoint/Excel 之間共用，而且可以在任一應用程式中設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1023">This setting is shared across Outlook/Word/PowerPoint/Excel and can be set in any of these apps.</span></span>

#### <a name="dedupe-mru-entries-when-using-the-onedrive-sync-client"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-1096">使用 OneDrive 同步處理用戶端時的刪除重複資料 MRU 項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1096">Dedupe MRU entries when using the Onedrive sync client</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-1097">透過刪除重複資料 MRU 項目，改善 OneDrive 同步處理用戶端與雲端附件的整合度並加快附加速度，讓其速度足以媲美同步處理資料的複製行為</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1097">Enable better integration with onedrive sync client with cloud attachments by deduping the mru entries and to enable faster attach as copy behavior for synchronized data</span></span>

##### <a name="getting-started"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-1098">開始使用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1098">Getting Started:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-1099">若您使用的是 OneDrive 同步處理用戶端，將再也看不到「附加檔案 MRU」的檔案重複項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1099">If you use the OneDrive sync client, you will no longer see file duplicates in the Attach File MRU.</span></span>

##### <a name="scenarios-to-try"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-1100">可嘗試使用的案例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1100">Scenarios to Try:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-1101">啟用 OneDrive 同步處理用戶端，並使用 Outlook 電腦版的 [附加檔案] 功能表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1101">Enable the OneDrive sync client and use the Attach File menu in Outlook Desktop</span></span>

#### <a name="improved-shared-folder-synchronization-for-mailboxes-with-many-folders"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-1102">已改善擁有多個資料夾的信箱共用資料夾同步處理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1102">Improved shared folder synchronization for mailboxes with many folders</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-1103">Outlook 多年來在同步共用信箱時，其資料夾的數量限制最多為 500 個。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1103">For years Outlook has been limited to a maximum of 500 folders when synchronizing shared mailboxes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-1104">透過這項變更已讓 Outlook 獲得改善，您在同步時將不會再遇到這 500 個資料夾的數量限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1104">With this change Outlook has been improved to sync in a way that will no longer encounter this 500 folder limit.</span></span>

##### <a name="getting-started"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-1105">開始使用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1105">Getting Started:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-1106">在信箱中新增 1000 個資料夾、讓其他人存取信箱、新增「其他人」的 Outlook 設定檔，然後確認同步處理是否可正常運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1106">Create 1000 folders in a mailbox, give someone else access to the mailbox, create an Outlook profile for the "someone else" and verify that sync works.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-1270">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1270">Outlook</span></span>

#### <a name="outlook-for-windows--set-and-share-your-focused-inbox-settings"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-1271">Windows 版 Outlook：設定並共用您的 [焦點收件匣] 設定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1271">Outlook for Windows:  set and share your Focused Inbox settings</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-1272">[焦點收件匣] 喜好設定會儲存在雲端內，因此當您在任何電腦上使用 Windows 版 Outlook 和 Outlook 網頁版時，都可以取得相同的一致體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1272">Your Focused Inbox preferences are stored in the cloud so you can enjoy the same consistent experience when using Outlook for Windows and Outlook on the web on any computer.</span></span>

#### <a name="getting-started"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-1273">開始使用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1273">Getting Started:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-1274">在 [檔案] > [選項] > [一般] 索引標籤下，還有一個名為 [將我的 Outlook 設定儲存在雲端中] 的新喜好設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1274">Under File > Options > General tab, there is a new preference for 'Store my Outlook settings in the cloud'.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-1275">使用者需要核取方塊，才能讓他們的 [焦點收件匣] 設定漫遊到其他電腦的 Outlook 安裝和 OWA。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1275">Users will need to check the box to enable their Focused Inbox setting to roam to other Desktop Outlook installations and OWA.</span></span>

#### <a name="scenarios-to-try"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-1276">可嘗試使用的案例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1276">Scenarios to Try:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-1277">在已開啟雲端設定喜好設定的電腦上變更 [焦點收件匣]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1277">Change Focused Inbox on the machine that has cloud settings preference turned on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-1278">瀏覽至 OWA，然後查看那裡也同樣套用了喜好設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1278">Navigate to OWA and see the preference applied there as well.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-1279">在 OWA 變更 [焦點收件匣]，然後啟動電腦版 Outlook 查看已反映喜好設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1279">Change Focused Inbox in OWA and start Desktop Outlook to see the preference reflected.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-1280">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1280">Word</span></span>

#### <a name="learning-tools-mode-has-additional-support-for-more-page-colors"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-1281">[學習工具] 模式額外支援更多頁面色彩</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1281">Learning Tools mode has additional support for more page colors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-1282">Word 中的 [學習工具] 新增更多頁面佈景主題色彩的支援，讓您能夠變更頁面的背景色彩。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1282">Learning Tools in Word adds support for more page theme colors, which allows the changing of the background color of the page.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="62973-1283">許多人在背景全白或全黑時閱讀會有困難，因此我們在 PC 和 Mac 的 Word 中增加了色彩選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1283">Many people have challenges reading with an all-white or all-black background, so we’ve expanded the choice of colors in Word on PC and Mac.</span></span>

#### <a name="getting-started"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-1284">開始使用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1284">Getting Started:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="62973-1450">選取要轉化的圖形</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1450">Specify the shapes you want to morph</span></span>

#### <a name="getting-started"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-1451">開始使用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1451">Getting Started:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="62973-1452">若要使轉化將兩個物件視為同一個物件，使用者可以使用 [選取窗格] 重新命名圖形。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1452">To get Morph to treat two objects as the same object, the user can rename the shapes using the Selection Pane.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="62973-1453">名稱前面必須加上「!!」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1453">The name must be prefaced with “!!”</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-1454">(兩個半形驚嘆號)，例如「!!名稱」，轉化才能用來覆寫預設比對行為</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1454">(two exclamation points) for Morph to use it to override our default matching behavior, e.g. “!!Name”</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="62973-1455">使用者可以繼續將圖形重新命名為不是以「!!」為開頭的任何名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1455">Users can continue to rename shapes with any name that doesn’t start with “!!”</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="62973-1456">不必擔心會變更轉化的運作方式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1456">without worrying that it will change the way Morph works</span></span>

#### <a name="scenarios-to-try"></a><span data-ttu-id="62973-1457">可嘗試使用的案例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1457">Scenarios to Try:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="62973-1460">在第 2 張投影片中插入不同的圖形，讓我們假設是三角形</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1460">Insert a different shape in the 2nd slide, let's say Triangle</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="62973-1461">開啟 [選取窗格]，將投影片 1 中的矩形重新命名為「!!圖形」，將投影片 2 中的三角形重新命名為「!!圖形」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="62973-1461">Open SelectionPane, rename the Rectangle in slide 1 to "!!shape", and rename the Triangle in slide 2 to "!!shape"</span></span>
